360	    @pytest.mark.parametrize(
361	        "required_param",
362	        [
363	            "issuer",
364	            "authorization_endpoint",
365	            "jwks_uri",
366	            "response_types_supported",
367	            "subject_types_supported",
368	            "id_token_signing_alg_values_supported",
369	        ],
370	    )
371	    def test_required_parameters(self, required_param):
372	        provider_config = {
373	            "issuer": "https://server.example.com",
374	            "authorization_endpoint": "https://server.example.com/connect/authorize",
375	            "jwks_uri": "https://server.example.com/jwks.json",
376	            "response_types_supported": [
377	                "code",
378	                "code id_token",
379	                "id_token",
380	                "token id_token",
381	            ],
382	            "subject_types_supported": ["public", "pairwise"],
383	            "id_token_signing_alg_values_supported": ["RS256", "ES256", "HS256"],
384	        }
385	
386	        del provider_config[required_param]
387	        with pytest.raises(MissingRequiredAttribute):
388	            ProviderConfigurationResponse(**provider_config).verify()
389	
390	    def test_token_endpoint_is_not_required_for_implicit_flow_only(self):
391	        provider_config = {
392	            "issuer": "https://server.example.com",
393	            "authorization_endpoint": "https://server.example.com/connect/authorize",
394	            "jwks_uri": "https://server.example.com/jwks.json",
